runners/core-construction-java module no longer exists as a separate directory under runners/. Its content was migrated into sdks/java/core/src/main/java/org/apache/beam/sdk/util/construction/ and sdks/java/core/src/main/java/org/apache/beam/sdk/runners/. The runners/core-java/ module still exists and contains execution primitives (DoFnRunner, StateInternals, etc.) along with a stub construction package (SerializablePipelineOptions.java). The five key translation concepts map to the following files:\\n\\n1. PipelineTranslator interface: The canonical translation mechanism is Pipeline.PipelineVisitor (an interface defined inside sdks/java/core/src/main/java/org/apache/beam/sdk/Pipeline.java). Runner-specific translators (e.g., FlinkPipelineTranslator, DataflowPipelineTranslator, Spark's PipelineTranslator) extend Pipeline.PipelineVisitor.Defaults and call pipeline.traverseTopologically(this) to walk the graph.\\n\\n2. TransformHierarchy walker: sdks/java/core/src/main/java/org/apache/beam/sdk/runners/TransformHierarchy.java — class TransformHierarchy. It tracks composite and primitive transforms, their inputs/outputs, and is traversed topologically during pipeline translation. It supports applyOverrides() to inject PTransformOverride replacements.\\n\\n3. PTransformOverride mechanism: Three files work together — sdks/java/core/src/main/java/org/apache/beam/sdk/runners/PTransformOverride.java (value class PTransformOverride pairing a PTransformMatcher with a PTransformOverrideFactory), sdks/java/core/src/main/java/org/apache/beam/sdk/runners/PTransformOverrideFactory.java (interface for producing replacement transforms), and sdks/java/core/src/main/java/org/apache/beam/sdk/runners/PTransformMatcher.java (functional interface for matching transforms to override). Runners call Pipeline.replaceAll(List<PTransformOverride>) before translation.\\n\\n4. ExecutableStagePayload construction: sdks/java/core/src/main/java/org/apache/beam/sdk/util/construction/graph/ExecutableStage.java defines the ExecutableStage interface (URN beam:runner:executable_stage:v1) and its toPayload() method that produces RunnerApi.ExecutableStagePayload. sdks/java/core/src/main/java/org/apache/beam/sdk/util/construction/graph/ImmutableExecutableStage.java is the concrete @AutoValue implementation that constructs the payload. sdks/java/core/src/main/java/org/apache/beam/sdk/util/construction/ExecutableStageTranslation.java provides static helpers (getExecutableStagePayload, generateNameFromStagePayload) for extracting and naming ExecutableStagePayload from applied transforms.\\n\\n5. BoundedSource/UnboundedSource adapter classes: sdks/java/core/src/main/java/org/apache/beam/sdk/util/construction/UnboundedReadFromBoundedSource.java — class UnboundedReadFromBoundedSource — is a PTransform adapter that wraps a BoundedSource as an UnboundedSource, enabling bounded sources to run in streaming pipelines. sdks/java/core/src/main/java/org/apache/beam/sdk/util/construction/SplittableParDo.java contains the inner classes PrimitiveBoundedRead and PrimitiveUnboundedRead, which are the canonical runner-visible primitives for reading from BoundedSource and UnboundedSource respectively; SplittableParDo.convertReadBasedSplittableDoFnsToPrimitiveReadsIfNecessary() inserts the BoundedReadOverrideFactory/UnboundedReadOverrideFactory overrides. sdks/java/core/src/main/java/org/apache/beam/sdk/util/construction/ReadTranslation.java serializes PrimitiveBoundedRead and PrimitiveUnboundedRead transforms to RunnerApi.ReadPayload proto (used by portable runners).\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
